name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Discount Single Room
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Business travelers
info:40 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted March 27, 2024
msg:First of all, the overall situation is that it meets the standards of a 4-star hotel (not a 5-star hotel, some reviews are misleading, and the hotel description in the room also says 5-star standards). The hotel is relatively old, and some facilities are a bit old (such as the TV). The current price is still quite suitable. If the price is higher, it is not worth choosing. The training of some service staff needs to be strengthened. Here are the details
Advantages
Lobby: Very grand and spacious, which is no less than a 5-star hotel.
Sanitation: No particularly obvious sanitation problems were found, and the cleaning was OK.
Room: It is relatively spacious. For more photos, just look at the hotel description, which basically meets the standards.
Breakfast: Very good, with many options, both Chinese and Western, in line with 4-star standards, but definitely not enough for 5-star standards.
Service: The waiters in the restaurant are very diligent, and empty plates and the like are quickly taken away. Very busy
Small details: A lot of small items are provided, which may be useful when you are away from home. Snacks were given when checking in. To be honest, it would be better to give fruits. I looked at the ingredient list and it was a short essay.

Disadvantages, problems, suggestions:
Front desk: When checking in, a receptionist at the front desk was looking at his phone. Because I didn't see the phone screen, it was hard to say whether it was a work phone or a personal phone. In the past, other hotels have also encountered front desk staff replying to things on their phones, but basically they put down their phones before approaching the front desk. This time it was not the case. I walked to the front desk and knocked on the counter with my ID card before I realized that there was a guest. Another front desk was receiving other guests at this time. Even if it was a work phone, he was watching it attentively.
Facilities: When booking online, there was a swimming pool and a gym, but I didn't see it in the floor description of Building A. I didn't go to Building B, so I'm not sure if there is one. The front desk staff didn't introduce it, and there was no relevant content in the hotel description in the room (I read it twice). Other comments said that it was an outsourced swimming pool, but at least let the guests know.
Room: The cheap room was booked because of the structure of the building. It was located in the arc shape of the building, so the room layout was very awkward. There was a bathroom on the right hand side of the door (very spacious), but opposite the door was a long corridor, which was very depressing. Because of the arc shape, and the neatness of the bathroom, the room layout was awkward.
There was a gap at the top of the door, which affected the sound insulation a little, but the overall sound insulation of the room was still very good.
Breakfast: As mentioned before, it was very rich, but because it had to take into account both Chinese and Western styles, but the variety was not as much as that of a five-star hotel, resulting in a variety of foods, but not many choices in each category, and the overall matching was not very reasonable, and the proportion of staple foods was a bit large. There was another problem. There was no coffee cup for freshly ground coffee. Drinking beverages was in this glass cup, which was a bit hot to drink hot drinks. I looked for it, but I couldn't find a coffee cup, and there was more than one person looking for a cup.
Service: Except for the restaurant waiter, none of the other waiters greeted the guests when they met them, which was even worse than some express hotels.
Finally, if the price does not increase or even if there are other discounts, I will still choose this hotel when I go to Hefei. Next time I stay, I hope to see some improvements in details. The age of the hotel is not a problem. If it is well maintained and the details are thoughtful, it can still be very good.
